PER_Iranian_elections_decision_category = {
	PER_auto_update_gui_weekly = {
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = { hidden_trigger = { has_country_flag = PER_turn_off_IR_stuff } }
		fire_only_once = no
		is_good = yes
		selectable_mission = no
		days_mission_timeout = 7

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = PER }
				hidden_effect = {
					PER_scripted_effect_update_principalists_popularity_variable = yes
					if = { #8th Period
						limit = {
							date > 2001.6.1
							date < 2002.7.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.9
							}
						}
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_country_flag = PER_yazdi_goes
								}
								country_event = {
									id = PER_election_events.81
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { has_country_flag = PER_yazdi_goes }
								}
								country_event = {
									id = PER_election_events.8
								}
							}
						}

					}
					else_if = { #9th Period
						limit = {
							date > 2005.6.9
							date < 2006.7.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.11
							}
						}
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_country_flag = PER_kavakebian_goes
								}
								country_event = {
									id = PER_election_events.101
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { has_country_flag = PER_kavakebian_goes }
								}
								country_event = {
									id = PER_election_events.10
								}
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = { #10th Period
						limit = {
							date > 2009.6.5
							date < 2010.7.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.13
							}
						}
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_country_flag = PER_karroubi_goes
								}
								country_event = {
									id = PER_election_events.121
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { has_country_flag = PER_karroubi_goes }
								}
								country_event = {
									id = PER_election_events.12
								}
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = { #11th Period
						limit = {
							date > 2013.6.7
							date < 2014.7.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_country_flag = principalist_portrait_ghalibaf
									NOT = {
										has_country_flag = PER_mashaei_goes
									}
								}
								country_event = {
									id = PER_election_events.15
								}
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = {
									has_country_flag = PER_mashaei_goes
								}
								country_event = {
									id = PER_election_events.151
								}
							}
							else = {
								country_event = {
									id = PER_election_events.16
								}
							}
						}
						else = {
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.14
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = { #12th Period
						limit = {
							date > 2017.5.12
							date < 2018.6.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_country_flag = PER_bayadi_goes
								}
								country_event = {
									id = PER_election_events.181
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = {
										has_country_flag = PER_bayadi_goes
									}
								}
								country_event = {
									id = PER_election_events.18
								}
							}
						}
						else = {
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.17
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = { #13th Period
						limit = {
							date > 2021.6.11
							date < 2022.7.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.20
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								has_country_flag = PER_haghshenas_goes
							}
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.191
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									has_country_flag = PER_haghshenas_goes
								}
							}
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.19
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = { #14th Period
					limit = {
						date > 2024.6.5
						date < 2025.7.1
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = {
								var = principalists_popularity_percent
								value = 50
								compare = greater_than_or_equals
							}
						}
						country_event = {
							id = PER_election_events.201
						}
					}
					else = {
						country_event = {
							id = PER_election_events.202
						}
					}
				}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = PER_election_enabled
						}
						activate_mission = PER_auto_update_gui_weekly
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	PER_endorse_a_candidate = {

	#Principalists
	PER_the_new_phase_of_economic_plans = { # Principalists
		allowed = { tag = PER }

		icon = null
		days_re_enable = 180
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = PER_presidential_decisions_only_one_is_available_TT

					has_decision = PER_check_on_peoples_situation

		}

		complete_effect = {
			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 3 }
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_the_new_phase_of_economic_plans"
			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = -3 }

		ai_will_do = {

		}

	PER_economic_backup = {
		allowed = { original_tag = PER }
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 12
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = PER_econ_backup
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = stable_growth
					has_idea = fast_growth
					has_idea = economic_boom
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_economic_backup"

					has_idea = depression
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = depression
					add_idea = stable_growth
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = recession
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = recession
					add_idea = stable_growth
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = stagnation
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = stagnation
					add_idea = stable_growth
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}

# Have at least 5 Sattelites in space
# Control Musandam

				}

					amount = -10000
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = nuclear_missile_equipment_3

PER_clergy_balance_of_power_category = {
	PER_seda_o_sima_campaign = {
		allowed = { original_tag = PER }

		days_remove = 40

		days_re_enable = 130

		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = PER_doing_decision_z
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_seda_o_sima_campaign"
			set_country_flag = PER_doing_decision_z
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_seda_o_sima_campaign"
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = PER_clergy_balance_of_power_category
				value = 0.05
			}
			newline = yes
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.025 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.015 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			clr_country_flag = PER_doing_decision_z
		}

		modifier = {
			political_power_cost = 1
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}
